I have used Turo for over 2 years and there have been some ups and downs but overall it's a great alternative to the traditional rental car centers. Turo has been called the Airbnb of car rentals.

You can get a unique type of vehicle at a great rate from the person who actually owns the car instead of a large corporation.

Turo makes it easy to get approved online to rent a vehicle all you have to do is be over 21, have a valid driver's license (even from another country), and a credit / debit card.
Use this link to join Turo and you will get $25 off your first trip: JoinTuro. com

The cars available to choose from range from exotics, convertibles, sports cars, Jeeps, Tesla's, SUVs, trucks, luxury cars, eco-friendly, all electric, and minivans. All types of cool and different cars that you normally can't rent from a big RAC agency.

Turo makes it easy for almost anyone to rent a cool car. Check out the 100's of cars available in your area and also you will see the reviews on the vehicle and the host who owns the car. This way you know you're going to get a great vehicle from a reliable owner.</review>

<GmapID>0x80dcac59b3dbd3af:0x1991ab449bda301a<//GmapID>< Review>
We've lived here more than two and a half years and love it. I couldn't believe some of the reviews that were posted here. We've never had issues with infestations of any kind, and the few problems we've had during our stay have been handled promptly and professionally by the staff and management. The maintenance team is diligent and thorough, and everyone in the office is friendly and takes great care of us.

Also, to address the complaint about being billed twice for trash, one is for access to the dumpsters and one is to have trash (and recyclables) picked up from your door by a valet five nights a week. It's a wonderful convenience and we frequently use both services, so the separate and reasonable charges are fine by us.

We have been so happy here and so well cared for. We highly recommend Alvista Terrace. Rent hikes are happening all over, they can't be avoided, and what you'll pay here is well worth the space and service. We'll live here until we're ready to move out of state, and then we'll be sad to leave.< /Review>
